"mtk1">configured&nbsp;with&nbsp;a&nbsp;`responseSchema`&nbsp;to&nbsp;ensur=

>matches&nbsp;the&nbsp;application's&nbsp;TypeScript&nbsp;types.</span></sp=

p;</span><span class=3D"mtk1">received,&nbsp;it's&nbsp;presented&nbsp;in&nb=
sp;two&nbsp;user-friendly&nbsp;</span><span class=3D"mtk1">views:</span></s=
pan></div><div style=3D"top:352px;height:16px;" class=3D"view-line"><span><=

;this&nbsp;goal&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;Google&nbsp;Gemini&nbsp;</span><span =
